CREATE DATABASE kms;

USE kms;

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `answers` (
  `AnswerID` bigint(20) unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `UserID` int(10) unsigned NOT NULL,
  `QuestionID` bigint(20) unsigned NOT NULL,
  `AnswerDate` datetime NOT NULL,
  `Answer` text NOT NULL,
  `Best` enum('0','1') NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  PRIMARY KEY (`AnswerID`),
  KEY `fk_answers_questions` (`QuestionID`),
  KEY `fk_answers_users` (`UserID`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB  DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 AUTO_INCREMENT=14 ;

It needs Snapshot Isolation, which you are already using.&lt;/p&gt;\r\n\r\n&lt;p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; clear: both; word-wrap: break-word; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Arial, ''Liberation Sans'', ''DejaVu Sans'', sans-serif; line-height: 18px;"&gt;Because your trigger is running in your parent transaction, and your snapshot has become out of date, your whole transaction would need to start again. If this is a complex workload, maintaining this last updated data in this way would be costly.&lt;/p&gt;\r\n', '0');

It offers pretty good security. If you have code on this right now, I wouldn&amp;#39;t be in a rush to get off it. It&amp;#39;s adequate for most usages. But with that said, there are far better alternatives if you were starting a new project that I wouldn&amp;#39;t pick it.&lt;/p&gt;\r\n\r\n&lt;h1 style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-left: 0px; border: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Arial, ''Liberation Sans'', ''DejaVu Sans'', sans-serif; line-height: 18px;"&gt;\r\n	&lt;li style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: transparent; word-wrap: break-word;"&gt;\r\n	&lt;p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: transparent; clear: both; word-wrap: break-word;"&gt;Relative To&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/PBKDF2" style="margin: 0px; border: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: rgb(238, 238, 238); font-family: Consolas, Menlo, Monaco, ''Lucida Console'', ''Liberation Mono'', ''DejaVu Sans Mono'', ''Bitstream Vera Sans Mono'', ''Courier New'', monospace, serif;"&gt;pbkdf2&lt;/code&gt;&lt;/a&gt;: The&amp;nbsp;&lt;code style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: transparent; color: rgb(74, 107, 130); text-decoration: none; cursor: pointer;"&gt;&lt;code style="margin: 0px; padding: 1px 5px; border: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: rgb(238, 238, 238); font-family: Consolas, Menlo, Monaco, ''Lucida Console'', ''Liberation Mono'', ''DejaVu Sans Mono'', ''Bitstream Vera Sans Mono'', ''Courier New'', monospace, serif;"&gt;hash()&lt;/code&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;where&amp;nbsp;&lt;code style="margin: 0px; padding: 1px 5px; border: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: rgb(238, 238, 238); font-family: Consolas, Menlo, Monaco, ''Lucida Console'', ''Liberation Mono'', ''DejaVu Sans Mono'', ''Bitstream Vera Sans Mono'', ''Courier New'', monospace, serif;"&gt;pbkdf2()&lt;/code&gt;&amp;nbsp;uses&lt;a href="http://www.php.net/hash_hmac" style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: transparent; color: rgb(74, 107, 130); text-decoration: none; cursor: pointer;"&gt;&lt;code style="margin: 0px; padding: 1px 5px; border: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: rgb(238, 238, 238); font-family: Consolas, Menlo, Monaco, ''Lucida Console'', ''Liberation Mono'', ''DejaVu Sans Mono'', ''Bitstream Vera Sans Mono'', ''Courier New'', monospace, serif;"&gt;hash_hmac()&lt;/code&gt;&lt;/a&gt;. Now, a&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hash-based_message_authentication_code" style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: transparent; color: rgb(74, 107, 130); text-decoration: none; cursor: pointer;"&gt;HMAC&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;runs 2 hashes for every call internally, but the PHP implementation only takes approximately 1.6 times the execution of a single call to&amp;nbsp;&lt;code style="margin: 0px; padding: 1px 5px; border: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: rgb(238, 238, 238); font-family: Consolas, Menlo, Monaco, ''Lucida Console'', ''Liberation Mono'', ''DejaVu Sans Mono'', ''Bitstream Vera Sans Mono'', ''Courier New'', monospace, serif;"&gt;hash()&lt;/code&gt;&amp;nbsp;(isn&amp;#39;t C wonderful?). So we get 2 hashes from&amp;nbsp;&lt;code style="margin: 0px; padding: 1px 5px; border: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: rgb(238, 238, 238); font-family: Consolas, Menlo, Monaco, ''Lucida Console'', ''Liberation Mono'', ''DejaVu Sans Mono'', ''Bitstream Vera Sans Mono'', ''Courier New'', monospace, serif;"&gt;hash_hmac&lt;/code&gt;&amp;nbsp;in 62% of the time it would take&amp;nbsp;&lt;code style="margin: 0px; padding: 1px 5px; border: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: rgb(238, 238, 238); font-family: Consolas, Menlo, Monaco, ''Lucida Console'', ''Liberation Mono'', ''DejaVu Sans Mono'', ''Bitstream Vera Sans Mono'', ''Courier New'', monospace, serif;"&gt;hash()&lt;/code&gt;&amp;nbsp;to execute 2 hashes.&lt;/p&gt;\r\n\r\n	&lt;p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: transparent; clear: both; word-wrap: break-word;"&gt;What does that mean? Well, for&amp;nbsp;&lt;em style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: transparent;"&gt;a given runtime&lt;/em&gt;,&amp;nbsp;&lt;code style="margin: 0px; padding: 1px 5px; border: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: rgb(238, 238, 238); font-family: Consolas, Menlo, Monaco, ''Lucida Console'', ''Liberation Mono'', ''DejaVu Sans Mono'', ''Bitstream Vera Sans Mono'', ''Courier New'', monospace, serif;"&gt;pbkdf2&lt;/code&gt;&amp;nbsp;will run approximately 37.5%&amp;nbsp;&lt;strong style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: transparent;"&gt;more&lt;/strong&gt;hashes than the&amp;nbsp;&lt;code style="margin: 0px; padding: 1px 5px; border: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: rgb(238, 238, 238); font-family: Consolas, Menlo, Monaco, ''Lucida Console'', ''Liberation Mono'', ''DejaVu Sans Mono'', ''Bitstream Vera Sans Mono'', ''Courier New'', monospace, serif;"&gt;phpass&lt;/code&gt;&amp;nbsp;algorithm. More hashes in a given time == good, because it results in more computation being performed.&lt;/p&gt;\r\n\r\n	&lt;p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: transparent; clear: both; word-wrap: break-word;"&gt;So&amp;nbsp;&lt;code style="margin: 0px; padding: 1px 5px; border: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: rgb(238, 238, 238); font-family: Consolas, Menlo, Monaco, ''Lucida Console'', ''Liberation Mono'', ''DejaVu Sans Mono'', ''Bitstream Vera Sans Mono'', ''Courier New'', monospace, serif;"&gt;pbkdf2&lt;/code&gt;&amp;nbsp;is approximately&amp;nbsp;&lt;code style="margin: 0px; padding: 1px 5px; border: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: rgb(238, 238, 238); font-family: Consolas, Menlo, Monaco, ''Lucida Console'', ''Liberation Mono'', ''DejaVu Sans Mono'', ''Bitstream Vera Sans Mono'', ''Courier New'', monospace, serif;"&gt;37.5%&lt;/code&gt;&amp;nbsp;stronger than&amp;nbsp;&lt;code style="margin: 0px; padding: 1px 5px; border: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: rgb(238, 238, 238); font-family: Consolas, Menlo, Monaco, ''Lucida Console'', ''Liberation Mono'', ''DejaVu Sans Mono'', ''Bitstream Vera Sans Mono'', ''Courier New'', monospace, serif;"&gt;phpass&lt;/code&gt;&amp;nbsp;when using the same primitive (&lt;code style="margin: 0px; padding: 1px 5px; border: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: rgb(238, 238, 238); font-family: Consolas, Menlo, Monaco, ''Lucida Console'', ''Liberation Mono'', ''DejaVu Sans Mono'', ''Bitstream Vera Sans Mono'', ''Courier New'', monospace, serif;"&gt;md5&lt;/code&gt;in this case). But&amp;nbsp;&lt;code style="margin: 0px; padding: 1px 5px; border: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: rgb(238, 238, 238); font-family: Consolas, Menlo, Monaco, ''Lucida Console'', ''Liberation Mono'', ''DejaVu Sans Mono'', ''Bitstream Vera Sans Mono'', ''Courier New'', monospace, serif;"&gt;pbkdf2&lt;/code&gt;&amp;nbsp;can also take stronger primitives. So we can use&amp;nbsp;&lt;code style="margin: 0px; padding: 1px 5px; border: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: rgb(238, 238, 238); font-family: Consolas, Menlo, Monaco, ''Lucida Console'', ''Liberation Mono'', ''DejaVu Sans Mono'', ''Bitstream Vera Sans Mono'', ''Courier New'', monospace, serif;"&gt;pbkdf2&lt;/code&gt;&amp;nbsp;with&amp;nbsp;&lt;code style="margin: 0px; padding: 1px 5px; border: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: rgb(238, 238, 238); font-family: Consolas, Menlo, Monaco, ''Lucida Console'', ''Liberation Mono'', ''DejaVu Sans Mono'', ''Bitstream Vera Sans Mono'', ''Courier New'', monospace, serif;"&gt;sha512&lt;/code&gt;to gain a very significant advantage over the&amp;nbsp;&lt;code style="margin: 0px; padding: 1px 5px; border: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: rgb(238, 238, 238); font-family: Consolas, Menlo, Monaco, ''Lucida Console'', ''Liberation Mono'', ''DejaVu Sans Mono'', ''Bitstream Vera Sans Mono'', ''Courier New'', monospace, serif;"&gt;phpass&lt;/code&gt;&amp;nbsp;algorithm (mainly because&amp;nbsp;&lt;code style="margin: 0px; padding: 1px 5px; border: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: rgb(238, 238, 238); font-family: Consolas, Menlo, Monaco, ''Lucida Console'', ''Liberation Mono'', ''DejaVu Sans Mono'', ''Bitstream Vera Sans Mono'', ''Courier New'', monospace, serif;"&gt;sha512&lt;/code&gt;&amp;nbsp;is a&lt;em style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: transparent;"&gt;harder&lt;/em&gt;&amp;nbsp;algorithm with more computation than&amp;nbsp;&lt;code style="margin: 0px; padding: 1px 5px; border: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: rgb(238, 238, 238); font-family: Consolas, Menlo, Monaco, ''Lucida Console'', ''Liberation Mono'', ''DejaVu Sans Mono'', ''Bitstream Vera Sans Mono'', ''Courier New'', monospace, serif;"&gt;md5&lt;/code&gt;).&lt;/p&gt;\r\n\r\n	&lt;p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: transparent; clear: both; word-wrap: break-word;"&gt;This means that not only is&amp;nbsp;&lt;code style="margin: 0px; padding: 1px 5px; border: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: rgb(238, 238, 238); font-family: Consolas, Menlo, Monaco, ''Lucida Console'', ''Liberation Mono'', ''DejaVu Sans Mono'', ''Bitstream Vera Sans Mono'', ''Courier New'', monospace, serif;"&gt;pbkdf2&lt;/code&gt;&amp;nbsp;able to generate more computations in the same amount of time, it&amp;#39;s able to generate&amp;nbsp;&lt;em style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: transparent;"&gt;harder&lt;/em&gt;&amp;nbsp;computations.&lt;/p&gt;\r\n\r\n	&lt;p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: transparent; clear: both; word-wrap: break-word;"&gt;With that said, the difference isn&amp;#39;t&amp;nbsp;&lt;em style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: transparent;"&gt;overly&lt;/em&gt;&amp;nbsp;significant. It&amp;#39;s very much measurable, and&amp;nbsp;&lt;code style="margin: 0px; padding: 1px 5px; border: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: rgb(238, 238, 238); font-family: Consolas, Menlo, Monaco, ''Lucida Console'', ''Liberation Mono'', ''DejaVu Sans Mono'', ''Bitstream Vera Sans Mono'', ''Courier New'', monospace, serif;"&gt;pbkdf2&lt;/code&gt;&amp;nbsp;is definitely &amp;quot;stronger&amp;quot; than&amp;nbsp;&lt;code style="margin: 0px; padding: 1px 5px; border: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: rgb(238, 238, 238); font-family: Consolas, Menlo, Monaco, ''Lucida Console'', ''Liberation Mono'', ''DejaVu Sans Mono'', ''Bitstream Vera Sans Mono'', ''Courier New'', monospace, serif;"&gt;phpass&lt;/code&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;\r\n	&lt;/li&gt;\r\n	&lt;li style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: transparent; word-wrap: break-word;"&gt;\r\n	&lt;p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: transparent; clear: both; word-wrap: break-word;"&gt;Relative To&amp;nbsp;&lt;code style="margin: 0px; padding: 1px 5px; border: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: rgb(238, 238, 238); font-family: Consolas, Menlo, Monaco, ''Lucida Console'', ''Liberation Mono'', ''DejaVu Sans Mono'', ''Bitstream Vera Sans Mono'', ''Courier New'', monospace, serif;"&gt;bcrypt&lt;/code&gt;: This is a lot harder of a comparison to make. But let&amp;#39;s look at the surface of it.&lt;code style="margin: 0px; padding: 1px 5px; border: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: rgb(238, 238, 238); font-family: Consolas, Menlo, Monaco, ''Lucida Console'', ''Liberation Mono'', ''DejaVu Sans Mono'', ''Bitstream Vera Sans Mono'', ''Courier New'', monospace, serif;"&gt;phpass&lt;/code&gt;&amp;nbsp;uses&amp;nbsp;&lt;code style="margin: 0px; padding: 1px 5px; border: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: rgb(238, 238, 238); font-family: Consolas, Menlo, Monaco, ''Lucida Console'', ''Liberation Mono'', ''DejaVu Sans Mono'', ''Bitstream Vera Sans Mono'', ''Courier New'', monospace, serif;"&gt;md5&lt;/code&gt;, and a loop in PHP.&amp;nbsp;&lt;code style="margin: 0px; padding: 1px 5px; border: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: rgb(238, 238, 238); font-family: Consolas, Menlo, Monaco, ''Lucida Console'', ''Liberation Mono'', ''DejaVu Sans Mono'', ''Bitstream Vera Sans Mono'', ''Courier New'', monospace, serif;"&gt;pbkdf2&lt;/code&gt;&amp;nbsp;uses any primitive (in C) and a loop in PHP.&lt;code style="margin: 0px; padding: 1px 5px; border: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: rgb(238, 238, 238); font-family: Consolas, Menlo, Monaco, ''Lucida Console'', ''Liberation Mono'', ''DejaVu Sans Mono'', ''Bitstream Vera Sans Mono'', ''Courier New'', monospace, serif;"&gt;bcrypt&lt;/code&gt;&amp;nbsp;uses a custom algorithm all in C (meaning it&amp;#39;s a different algorithm from any available hash). So right of the bat,&amp;nbsp;&lt;code style="margin: 0px; padding: 1px 5px; border: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: rgb(238, 238, 238); font-family: Consolas, Menlo, Monaco, ''Lucida Console'', ''Liberation Mono'', ''DejaVu Sans Mono'', ''Bitstream Vera Sans Mono'', ''Courier New'', monospace, serif;"&gt;bcrypt&lt;/code&gt;&amp;nbsp;has a significant advantage just do to the fact that the algorithm is all in C. This allows for more &amp;quot;computation&amp;quot; per unit time. Thereby making it a more efficient slow algorithm (more computations in the given runtime).&lt;/p&gt;\r\n\r\n	&lt;p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: transparent; clear: both; word-wrap: break-word;"&gt;But just as important as how many computations it does is the quality of the computations. This could an entire research paper, but in short it comes down to the fact that the computations that bcrypt uses internally are much harder to perform than a normal hash function.&lt;/p&gt;\r\n\r\n	&lt;p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: transparent; clear: both; word-wrap: break-word;"&gt;One example of the stronger nature of&amp;nbsp;&lt;code style="margin: 0px; padding: 1px 5px; border: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: rgb(238, 238, 238); font-family: Consolas, Menlo, Monaco, ''Lucida Console'', ''Liberation Mono'', ''DejaVu Sans Mono'', ''Bitstream Vera Sans Mono'', ''Courier New'', monospace, serif;"&gt;bcrypt&lt;/code&gt;&amp;nbsp;is the fact that&amp;nbsp;&lt;code style="margin: 0px; padding: 1px 5px; border: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: rgb(238, 238, 238); font-family: Consolas, Menlo, Monaco, ''Lucida Console'', ''Liberation Mono'', ''DejaVu Sans Mono'', ''Bitstream Vera Sans Mono'', ''Courier New'', monospace, serif;"&gt;bcrypt&lt;/code&gt;&amp;nbsp;uses a far larger internal state than a normal hash function.&amp;nbsp;&lt;code style="margin: 0px; padding: 1px 5px; border: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: rgb(238, 238, 238); font-family: Consolas, Menlo, Monaco, ''Lucida Console'', ''Liberation Mono'', ''DejaVu Sans Mono'', ''Bitstream Vera Sans Mono'', ''Courier New'', monospace, serif;"&gt;SHA512&lt;/code&gt;&amp;nbsp;uses a 512 bit internal state to compute against a block of 1024 bits.&amp;nbsp;&lt;code style="margin: 0px; padding: 1px 5px; border: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: rgb(238, 238, 238); font-family: Consolas, Menlo, Monaco, ''Lucida Console'', ''Liberation Mono'', ''DejaVu Sans Mono'', ''Bitstream Vera Sans Mono'', ''Courier New'', monospace, serif;"&gt;bcrypt&lt;/code&gt;&amp;nbsp;uses instead about 32kb of internal state to compute against a single block of 576 bits. The fact that&amp;nbsp;&lt;code style="margin: 0px; padding: 1px 5px; border: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: rgb(238, 238, 238); font-family: Consolas, Menlo, Monaco, ''Lucida Console'', ''Liberation Mono'', ''DejaVu Sans Mono'', ''Bitstream Vera Sans Mono'', ''Courier New'', monospace, serif;"&gt;bcrypt&lt;/code&gt;&amp;#39;s internal state is so much bigger than&amp;nbsp;&lt;code style="margin: 0px; padding: 1px 5px; border: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: rgb(238, 238, 238); font-family: Consolas, Menlo, Monaco, ''Lucida Console'', ''Liberation Mono'', ''DejaVu Sans Mono'', ''Bitstream Vera Sans Mono'', ''Courier New'', monospace, serif;"&gt;SHA512&lt;/code&gt;&amp;nbsp;(and&amp;nbsp;&lt;code style="margin: 0px; padding: 1px 5px; border: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: rgb(238, 238, 238); font-family: Consolas, Menlo, Monaco, ''Lucida Console'', ''Liberation Mono'', ''DejaVu Sans Mono'', ''Bitstream Vera Sans Mono'', ''Courier New'', monospace, serif;"&gt;md5&lt;/code&gt;&amp;nbsp;and&lt;code style="margin: 0px; padding: 1px 5px; border: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: rgb(238, 238, 238); font-family: Consolas, Menlo, Monaco, ''Lucida Console'', ''Liberation Mono'', ''DejaVu Sans Mono'', ''Bitstream Vera Sans Mono'', ''Courier New'', monospace, serif;"&gt;phpass&lt;/code&gt;) partially accounts for the stronger nature of&amp;nbsp;&lt;code style="margin: 0px; padding: 1px 5px; border: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: rgb(238, 238, 238); font-family: Consolas, Menlo, Monaco, ''Lucida Console'', ''Liberation Mono'', ''DejaVu Sans Mono'', ''Bitstream Vera Sans Mono'', ''Courier New'', monospace, serif;"&gt;bcrypt&lt;/code&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;\r\n	&lt;/li&gt;\r\n&lt;/ul&gt;\r\n\r\n&lt;h1 style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; font-family: ''Trebuchet MS'', ''Liberation Sans'', ''DejaVu Sans'', sans-serif; font-weight: bold; word-wrap: break-word; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 22px !important; line-height: 24px !important;"&gt;Should It Be Avoided&lt;/h1&gt;\r\n\r\n&lt;p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; clear: both; word-wrap: break-word; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Arial, ''Liberation Sans'', ''DejaVu Sans'', sans-serif; line-height: 18px;"&gt;For new projects,&amp;nbsp;&lt;strong style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: transparent;"&gt;absolutely&lt;/strong&gt;. It&amp;#39;s not that it&amp;#39;s bad. It isn&amp;#39;t. It&amp;#39;s that there are demonstrably stronger algorithms out there (by orders of magnitude). So why not use them?&lt;/p&gt;\r\n\r\n&lt;p style="margin: 0px 0px 1em; padding: 0px; border: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; clear: both; word-wrap: break-word; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: Arial, ''Liberation Sans'', ''DejaVu Sans'', sans-serif; line-height: 18px;"&gt;For further proof of how&amp;nbsp;&lt;code style="margin: 0px; padding: 1px 5px; border: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: rgb(238, 238, 238); font-family: Consolas, Menlo, Monaco, ''Lucida Console'', ''Liberation Mono'', ''DejaVu Sans Mono'', ''Bitstream Vera Sans Mono'', ''Courier New'', monospace, serif;"&gt;bcrypt&lt;/code&gt;&amp;nbsp;is stronger, check out the&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://passwords12.at.ifi.uio.no/Jeremi_Gosney_Password_Cracking_HPC_Passwords12.pdf" style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: transparent; color: rgb(74, 107, 130); text-decoration: none; cursor: pointer;"&gt;Slides from Password13 (PDF)&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;which launched a 25 GPU cluster for cracking password hashes. Here are the relevant results:&lt;/p&gt;\r\n\r\n&lt;ul style="margin: 0px 0px 1em 30px; padding-right: 0px; padding-left: 0px; border: 0px; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; list-style-position: initial;   `CategoryID` int(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `Name` varchar(200) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`CategoryID`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB  DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 AUTO_INCREMENT=7 ;

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `articles` (
  `ArticleID` bigint(20) unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `Title` varchar(100) NOT NULL,
  `Content` text NOT NULL,

  `CategoryID` INT(11),

  KEY `fk_articles_users` (`UserID`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB  DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 AUTO_INCREMENT=23 ;

Usually all of the interface hardware needed to operate the laptop, such as&amp;nbsp;&lt;a class="mw-redirect" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/USB" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="USB"&gt;USB ports&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;(previously&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Parallel_port" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Parallel port"&gt;parallel&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;and&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Serial_port" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Serial port"&gt;serial ports&lt;/a&gt;), graphics card, sound channel, etc., are built in to a single unit. Laptops contain high capacity&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Battery_(electricity)" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Battery (electricity)"&gt;batteries&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;that can power the device for extensive periods of time, enhancing portability. Once the battery charge is depleted, it will have to be recharged through a power outlet. In the interest of saving power, weight and space, they usually share RAM with the video channel, slowing their performance compared to an equivalent desktop machine. For this reason, Desktop or Gaming computers are generally preferred to laptop PCs for gaming purposes.&lt;/p&gt;\r\n\r\n&lt;p style="margin: 0.4em 0px 0.5em; line-height: 19.1875px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: sans-serif;"&gt;One main drawback of the laptop is sometimes, due to the size and configuration of components, relatively little can be done to upgrade the overall computer from its original design. Internal upgrades are either not manufacturer recommended, can damage the laptop if done with poor care or knowledge, or in some cases impossible, making the desktop PC more modular. Some internal upgrades, such as memory and hard disks upgrades are often easy, a display or keyboard upgrade is usually impossible. The laptop has the same access as the desktop to the wide variety of devices, such as external displays, mice, cameras, storage devices and keyboards, which may be attached externally through USB ports and other less common ports such as external video.&lt;/p&gt;\r\n\r\n&lt;p style="margin: 0.4em 0px 0.5em; line-height: 19.1875px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: sans-serif;"&gt;A subtype of notebooks, called&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Subnotebook" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Subnotebook"&gt;subnotebooks&lt;/a&gt;, are computers with most of the features of a standard laptop computer but smaller. (7, 'Hardware', '&lt;p style="margin: 0.4em 0px 0.5em; line-height: 19.1875px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: sans-serif;"&gt;Hardware is a comprehensive term for all of the physical parts of a computer, as distinguished from the data it contains or operates on, and the software that provides instructions for the hardware to accomplish tasks. The boundary between hardware and software is slightly blurry - firmware is software that is &amp;quot;built-in&amp;quot; to the hardware.&lt;/p&gt;\r\n\r\n&lt;p style="margin: 0.4em 0px 0.5em; line-height: 19.1875px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: sans-serif;"&gt;Mass-market consumer computers use highly standardized components and so are simple for an end user to assemble into a working system. A typical&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Desktop_computer" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Desktop computer"&gt;desktop computer&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;consists of a&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Computer_case" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Computer case"&gt;computer case&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;which holds the&amp;nbsp;&lt;a class="mw-redirect" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Computer_power_supply" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Computer power supply"&gt;power supply&lt;/a&gt;,&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Motherboard" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Motherboard"&gt;motherboard&lt;/a&gt;,&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hard_disk_drive" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Hard disk drive"&gt;hard disk&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;and often an&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Optical_disc_drive" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Optical disc drive"&gt;optical disc drive&lt;/a&gt;. External devices such as a&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Computer_monitor" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Computer monitor"&gt;computer monitor&lt;/a&gt;or&amp;nbsp;&lt;a class="mw-redirect" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Visual_display_unit" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Visual display unit"&gt;visual display unit&lt;/a&gt;,&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Computer_keyboard" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Computer keyboard"&gt;keyboard&lt;/a&gt;, and a&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Pointing_device" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Pointing device"&gt;pointing device&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;are usually found in a personal computer.&lt;/p&gt;\r\n\r\n&lt;p style="margin: 0.4em 0px 0.5em; line-height: 19.1875px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: sans-serif;"&gt;The motherboard connects all processor, memory and peripheral devices together. The&amp;nbsp;&lt;a class="mw-redirect" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/RAM" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="RAM"&gt;RAM&lt;/a&gt;, graphics card and processor are mounted directly onto the motherboard. The&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Central_processing_unit" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Central processing unit"&gt;central processing unit&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;microprocessor chip plugs into a&amp;nbsp;&lt;a class="mw-redirect" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cpu_socket" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Cpu socket"&gt;socket&lt;/a&gt;. Expansion memory plugs into memory sockets. Some motherboards have the video display adapter, sound and other peripherals integrated onto the motherboard, while others use&amp;nbsp;&lt;a class="mw-redirect" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Expansion_slot" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Expansion slot"&gt;expansion slots&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;for graphics cards, network cards, or other&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Input/output" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Input/output"&gt;I/O&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;devices. The graphics card or sound card may employ a&amp;nbsp;&lt;a class="mw-redirect" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Break_out_box" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Break out box"&gt;break out box&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;to keep the analog parts away from the&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Electromagnetic_radiation" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Electromagnetic radiation"&gt;electromagnetic radiation&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;inside the computer case. Disk drives for mass storage are connected to the mother board with a cable, and to the power supply through another cable. Usually disk drives are mounted in the same case as the motherboard; formerly, expansion chassis were made for additional disk storage. For really large amounts of data, a&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tape_drive" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Tape drive"&gt;tape drive&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;can be used or extra hard disks can be put together in an external case.&lt;/p&gt;\r\n\r\n&lt;p style="margin: 0.4em 0px 0.5em; line-height: 19.1875px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: sans-serif;"&gt;The keyboard and the mouse are external devices plugged into the computer through connectors on an I/O panel on the back of the computer. The monitor is also connected to the I/O panel, either through an onboard port on the motherboard, or a port on the graphics card.&lt;/p&gt;\r\n\r\n&lt;p style="margin: 0.4em 0px 0.5em; line-height: 19.1875px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: sans-serif;"&gt;The&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Computer_hardware" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Computer hardware"&gt;hardware&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;capabilities of personal computers can sometimes be extended by the addition of&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Expansion_card" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Expansion card"&gt;expansion cards&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;connected via an expansion&amp;nbsp;&lt;a class="mw-redirect" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Computer_bus" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Computer bus"&gt;bus&lt;/a&gt;. Some standard peripheral buses often used for adding expansion cards in personal computers as of 2005 are&amp;nbsp;&lt;a class="mw-redirect" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Peripheral_Component_Interconnect" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Peripheral Component Interconnect"&gt;PCI&lt;/a&gt;,&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Accelerated_Graphics_Port" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Accelerated Graphics Port"&gt;AGP&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;(a high-speed PCI bus dedicated to graphics adapters), and&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/PCI_Express" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="PCI Express"&gt;PCI Express&lt;/a&gt;. Most personal computers as of 2005 have multiple physical&amp;nbsp;&lt;a class="mw-redirect" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Peripheral_Component_Interconnect" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Peripheral Component Interconnect"&gt;PCI&lt;/a&gt;expansion slots. Many also include an AGP bus and expansion slot or a PCI Express bus and one or more expansion slots, but few PCs contain both buses.&lt;/p&gt;\r\n', 2, '2013-04-24 20:40:29'),
(8, 'Processor', '&lt;p style="margin: 0.4em 0px 0.5em; line-height: 19.1875px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: sans-serif;"&gt;The central processing unit, or CPU, is that part of a computer which executes software&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Computer_program" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Computer program"&gt;program&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;instructions. In newer PCs the CPU is about a million transistors in one integrated circuit chip called the&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Microprocessor" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Microprocessor"&gt;microprocessor&lt;/a&gt;. The microprocessor plugs into the motherboard. The chip generates so much heat that the PC builder is required to attach a special cooling device to its surface. Modern CPUs are equipped with a&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Computer_fan" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; (13, 'Windows Presentation Foundation', '&lt;p style="margin: 0.4em 0px 0.5em; line-height: 19.1875px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: sans-serif;"&gt;Developed by&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Microsoft" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Microsoft"&gt;Microsoft&lt;/a&gt;, the&amp;nbsp;&lt;b&gt;Windows Presentation Foundation&lt;/b&gt;&amp;nbsp;(or&amp;nbsp;&lt;b&gt;WPF&lt;/b&gt;) is a&amp;nbsp;&lt;a class="mw-redirect" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Computer_software" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Computer software"&gt;computer-software&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;graphical subsystem for rendering user interfaces in Windows-based applications. WPF, previously known as &amp;quot;Avalon&amp;quot;, was initially released as part of&amp;nbsp;&lt;a class="mw-redirect" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/.NET_Framework_3.0" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title=".NET Framework 3.0"&gt;.NET Framework 3.0&lt;/a&gt;. Rather than relying on the older&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Graphics_Device_Interface" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Graphics Device Interface"&gt;GDI&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;subsystem, WPF uses&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/DirectX" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="DirectX"&gt;DirectX&lt;/a&gt;. WPF attempts to provide a consistent programming model for building applications and separates the user interface from&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Business_logic" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Business logic"&gt;business logic&lt;/a&gt;. It resembles similar&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/XML" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="XML"&gt;XML&lt;/a&gt;-oriented&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Object_model" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Object model"&gt;object models&lt;/a&gt;, such as those implemented in&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/XUL" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="XUL"&gt;XUL&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;and&amp;nbsp;&lt;a class="mw-redirect" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/SVG" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="SVG"&gt;SVG&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;\r\n\r\n&lt;p style="margin: 0.4em 0px 0.5em; line-height: 19.1875px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: sans-serif;"&gt;WPF employs&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Extensible_Application_Markup_Language" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Extensible Application Markup Language"&gt;XAML&lt;/a&gt;, an&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/XML" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="XML"&gt;XML&lt;/a&gt;-based language, to define and link various&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/User_interface" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="User interface"&gt;UI&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;elements.&lt;sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-1" style="line-height: 1em;"&gt;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Windows_Presentation_Foundation#cite_note-1" style="text-decoration: none; WPF aims to unify a number of common&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/User_interface" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="User interface"&gt;user interface&lt;/a&gt;elements, such as 2D/3D rendering, fixed and adaptive&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Document_file_format" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Document file format"&gt;documents&lt;/a&gt;,&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Typography" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Typography"&gt;typography&lt;/a&gt;,&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vector_graphics" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Vector graphics"&gt;vector graphics&lt;/a&gt;, runtime&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Animation" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Animation"&gt;animation&lt;/a&gt;, and pre-rendered media. These elements can then be linked and manipulated based on various events, user interactions, and&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/XML_data_binding" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="XML data binding"&gt;data bindings&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;\r\n\r\n&lt;p style="margin: 0.4em 0px 0.5em; line-height: 19.1875px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: sans-serif;"&gt;WPF&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Runtime_library" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Runtime library"&gt;runtime libraries&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;are included with all versions of&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Microsoft_Windows" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Microsoft Windows"&gt;Microsoft Windows&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;since&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Windows_Vista" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Windows Vista"&gt;Windows Vista&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;and&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Windows_Server_2008" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Windows Server 2008"&gt;Windows Server 2008&lt;/a&gt;. color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; white-space: nowrap; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;"&gt;[5]&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/sup&gt;open source&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Relational_database_management_system" style="text-decoration: none; It is named after co-founder&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Michael_Widenius" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; line-height: 19.1875px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: sans-serif;"&gt;The MySQL development project has made its&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Source_code" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Proprietary software"&gt;proprietary&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;agreements. MySQL was owned and sponsored by a single&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Business" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Business"&gt;for-profit&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;firm, the&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sweden" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Oracle Corporation"&gt;Oracle Corporation&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-sunacquire_8-0" style="line-height: 1em;"&gt;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/MySQL#cite_note-sunacquire-8" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; white-space: nowrap; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;"&gt;[8]&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/sup&gt;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n\r\n&lt;p style="margin: 0.4em 0px 0.5em; line-height: 19.1875px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: sans-serif;"&gt;MySQL is a popular choice of database for use in web applications, and is a central component of the widely used&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/LAMP_(software_bundle)" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="LAMP (software bundle)"&gt;LAMP&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;open source web application software stack (and other&amp;nbsp;&lt;a class="mw-redirect" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/List_of_AMP_packages" style="text-decoration: none; LAMP is an acronym for &amp;quot;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Linux" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Linux"&gt;Linux&lt;/a&gt;,&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Apache_HTTP_Server" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Apache HTTP Server"&gt;Apache&lt;/a&gt;, MySQL,&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Perl" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Perl"&gt;Perl&lt;/a&gt;/&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/PHP" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="PHP"&gt;PHP&lt;/a&gt;/&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Python_(programming_language)" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Python (programming language)"&gt;Python&lt;/a&gt;.&amp;quot;&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Free_software" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Free software"&gt;Free-software&lt;/a&gt;-open source projects that require a full-featured database management system often use MySQL.&lt;/p&gt;\r\n\r\n&lt;p style="margin: 0.4em 0px 0.5em; line-height: 19.1875px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: sans-serif;"&gt;For commercial use, several paid editions are available, and offer additional functionality. color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; white-space: nowrap; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;"&gt;[7]&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/sup&gt;&amp;nbsp;or&amp;nbsp;&lt;span class="nowrap" style="white-space: nowrap;"&gt;&lt;span class="IPA" title="Representation in the International Phonetic Alphabet (IPA)"&gt;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:IPA_for_English" style="text-decoration: none !important; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Help:IPA for English"&gt;/&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class="IPA"&gt;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:IPA_for_English#Key" style="text-decoration: none !important; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Help:IPA for English"&gt;&lt;span style="border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: dotted;" title="/ˈ/ primary stress follows"&gt;ˈ&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class="IPA"&gt;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:IPA_for_English#Key" style="text-decoration: none !important; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Help:IPA for English"&gt;&lt;span style="border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: dotted;" title="''l'' in ''lie''"&gt;l&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class="IPA"&gt;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:IPA_for_English#Key" style="text-decoration: none !important; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Help:IPA for English"&gt;&lt;span style="border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: dotted;" title="/ɪ/ short ''i'' in ''bid''"&gt;ɪ&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class="IPA"&gt;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:IPA_for_English#Key" style="text-decoration: none !important; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Help:IPA for English"&gt;&lt;span style="border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: dotted;" title="''n'' in ''nigh''"&gt;n&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class="IPA"&gt;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:IPA_for_English#Key" style="text-decoration: none !important; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Help:IPA for English"&gt;&lt;span style="border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: dotted;" title="/ʊ/ short ''oo'' in ''foot''"&gt;ʊ&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class="IPA"&gt;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:IPA_for_English#Key" style="text-decoration: none !important; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Help:IPA for English"&gt;&lt;span style="border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: dotted;" title="''k'' in ''kind''"&gt;k&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class="IPA"&gt;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:IPA_for_English#Key" style="text-decoration: none !important; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Help:IPA for English"&gt;&lt;span style="border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-style: dotted;" title="''s'' in ''sigh''"&gt;s&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class="IPA" title="Representation in the International Phonetic Alphabet (IPA)"&gt;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:IPA_for_English" style="text-decoration: none !important; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Help:IPA for English"&gt;/&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;span class="Unicode" title="English pronunciation respelling"&gt;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wikipedia:Pronunciation_respelling_key" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Wikipedia:Pronunciation respelling key"&gt;&lt;i&gt;&lt;b&gt;&lt;span class="smallcaps"&gt;&lt;span class="SMALLCAPS" style="font-variant: small-caps;"&gt;&lt;span class="NOCAPS" style="text-transform: lowercase;"&gt;lin&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/b&gt;-uuks&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/span&gt;)&lt;sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-8" style="line-height: 1em;"&gt;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Linux#cite_note-8" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; white-space: nowrap; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;"&gt;[8]&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/sup&gt;&lt;sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-9" style="line-height: 1em;"&gt;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Linux#cite_note-9" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; white-space: nowrap; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;"&gt;[9]&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/sup&gt;&lt;sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-10" style="line-height: 1em;"&gt;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Linux#cite_note-10" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; white-space: nowrap; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;"&gt;[10]&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/sup&gt;&amp;nbsp;is a&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Unix-like" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Unix-like"&gt;Unix-like&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;computer&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Operating_system" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Operating system"&gt;operating system&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;assembled under the model of&amp;nbsp;&lt;a class="mw-redirect" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Free_and_open_source_software" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Free and open source software"&gt;free and open source software&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;development and distribution. The defining component of Linux is the&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Linux_kernel" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Linux kernel"&gt;Linux kernel&lt;/a&gt;,&lt;sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-11" style="line-height: 1em;"&gt;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Linux#cite_note-11" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; white-space: nowrap; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;"&gt;[11]&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/sup&gt;&amp;nbsp;an&amp;nbsp;&lt;a class="mw-redirect" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Operating_system_kernel" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Operating system kernel"&gt;operating system kernel&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;first released 5 October 1991 by&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Linus_Torvalds" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Linus Torvalds"&gt;Linus Torvalds&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-12" style="line-height: 1em;"&gt;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Linux#cite_note-12" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; white-space: nowrap; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;"&gt;[12]&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/sup&gt;&lt;sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-13" style="line-height: 1em;"&gt;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Linux#cite_note-13" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; white-space: nowrap; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;"&gt;[13]&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/sup&gt;&amp;nbsp;Since the main supporting&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/User_space" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="User space"&gt;user space&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;system tools and libraries originated in the&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/GNU_Project" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="GNU Project"&gt;GNU Project&lt;/a&gt;, initiated in 1983 by&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Richard_Stallman" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Richard Stallman"&gt;Richard Stallman&lt;/a&gt;, the&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Free_Software_Foundation" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Free Software Foundation"&gt;Free Software Foundation&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;prefers the name&amp;nbsp;&lt;i&gt;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/GNU/Linux_naming_controversy" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="GNU/Linux naming controversy"&gt;GNU/Linux&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/i&gt;.&lt;sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-lsag_14-0" style="line-height: 1em;"&gt;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Linux#cite_note-lsag-14" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; white-space: nowrap; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;"&gt;[14]&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/sup&gt;&lt;sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-gnu_homepage_15-0" style="line-height: 1em;"&gt;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Linux#cite_note-gnu_homepage-15" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; white-space: nowrap; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;"&gt;[15]&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/sup&gt;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n\r\n&lt;p style="margin: 0.4em 0px 0.5em; line-height: 19.1875px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: sans-serif;"&gt;Linux was originally developed as a free operating system for&amp;nbsp;&lt;a class="mw-redirect" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Intel_x86" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Intel x86"&gt;Intel x86&lt;/a&gt;-based personal computers. It has since been&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Porting" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Porting"&gt;ported&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;to more computer hardware platforms than any other operating system. It is a leading operating system on&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Server_(computing)" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Server (computing)"&gt;servers&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;and other&amp;nbsp;&lt;a class="mw-redirect" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Big_iron" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Big iron"&gt;big iron&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;systems such as&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mainframe_computer" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Mainframe computer"&gt;mainframe computers&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;and&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Supercomputer" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Supercomputer"&gt;supercomputers&lt;/a&gt;:&lt;sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-LinuxDevices_16-0" style="line-height: 1em;"&gt;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Linux#cite_note-LinuxDevices-16" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; white-space: nowrap; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;"&gt;[16]&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/sup&gt;&lt;sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-IBMLinuxWatch_17-0" style="line-height: 1em;"&gt;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Linux#cite_note-IBMLinuxWatch-17" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; white-space: nowrap; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;"&gt;[17]&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/sup&gt;&lt;sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-18" style="line-height: 1em;"&gt;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Linux#cite_note-18" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; white-space: nowrap; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;"&gt;[18]&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/sup&gt;&lt;sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-rules_supercomputers_19-0" style="line-height: 1em;"&gt;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Linux#cite_note-rules_supercomputers-19" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; white-space: nowrap; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;"&gt;[19]&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/sup&gt;&amp;nbsp;more than 90% of today&amp;#39;s&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/TOP500" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="TOP500"&gt;500 fastest supercomputers&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;run some variant of Linux,&lt;sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Top500_OS_list_20-0" style="line-height: 1em;"&gt;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Linux#cite_note-Top500_OS_list-20" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; white-space: nowrap; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;"&gt;[20]&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/sup&gt;&amp;nbsp;including the 10 fastest.&lt;sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-21" style="line-height: 1em;"&gt;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Linux#cite_note-21" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; white-space: nowrap; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;"&gt;[21]&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/sup&gt;&amp;nbsp;Linux also runs on&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Embedded_system" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Embedded system"&gt;embedded systems&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;(devices where the operating system is typically built into the&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Firmware" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Firmware"&gt;firmware&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;and highly tailored to the system) such as mobile phones,&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tablet_computer" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Tablet computer"&gt;tablet computers&lt;/a&gt;, network&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Router_(computing)" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Router (computing)"&gt;routers&lt;/a&gt;, building automation controls, televisions&lt;sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-22" style="line-height: 1em;"&gt;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Linux#cite_note-22" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; white-space: nowrap; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;"&gt;[22]&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/sup&gt;&lt;sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-23" style="line-height: 1em;"&gt;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Linux#cite_note-23" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; white-space: nowrap; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;"&gt;[23]&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/sup&gt;&amp;nbsp;and&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Video_game_console" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Video game console"&gt;video game consoles&lt;/a&gt;; the&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Android_(operating_system)" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Android (operating system)"&gt;Android&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;system in wide use on mobile devices is built on the Linux kernel.&lt;/p&gt;\r\n\r\n&lt;p style="margin: 0.4em 0px 0.5em; line-height: 19.1875px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: sans-serif;"&gt;The development of Linux is one of the most prominent examples of&amp;nbsp;&lt;a class="mw-redirect" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Free_and_open_source_software" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Free and open source software"&gt;free and open source software&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;collaboration: the underlying&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Source_code" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Source code"&gt;source code&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;may be used, modified, and distributed&amp;mdash;commercially or non-commercially&amp;mdash;by anyone under licenses such as the&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/GNU_General_Public_License" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="GNU General Public License"&gt;GNU General Public License&lt;/a&gt;. Typically Linux is packaged in a format known as a&amp;nbsp;&lt;i&gt;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Linux_distribution" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Linux distribution"&gt;Linux distribution&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/i&gt;&amp;nbsp;for desktop and server use. Some popular mainstream Linux distributions include&amp;nbsp;&lt;a class="mw-redirect" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Debian_(operating_system)" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Debian (operating system)"&gt;Debian&lt;/a&gt;(and its derivatives such as&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ubuntu_(operating_system)" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Ubuntu (operating system)"&gt;Ubuntu&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;and&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Linux_Mint" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Linux Mint"&gt;Linux Mint&lt;/a&gt;),&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Red_Hat_Enterprise_Linux" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Red Hat Enterprise Linux"&gt;Red Hat Enterprise Linux&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;(and its derivatives such as&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Fedora_(operating_system)" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Fedora (operating system)"&gt;Fedora&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;and&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/CentOS" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="CentOS"&gt;CentOS&lt;/a&gt;),&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mandriva_Linux" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Mandriva Linux"&gt;Mandriva&lt;/a&gt;/&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mageia" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Mageia"&gt;Mageia&lt;/a&gt;,&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OpenSUSE" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="OpenSUSE"&gt;openSUSE&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;(and its commercial derivative&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/SUSE_Linux_Enterprise_Server" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="SUSE Linux Enterprise Server"&gt;SUSE Linux Enterprise Server&lt;/a&gt;), and&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arch_Linux" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Arch Linux"&gt;Arch Linux&lt;/a&gt;. Linux distributions include the Linux kernel, supporting&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/System_software" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="System software"&gt;utilities&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;and&amp;nbsp;&lt;a class="mw-redirect" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Library_(computer_science)" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Library (computer science)"&gt;libraries&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;and usually a large amount of application software to fulfill the distribution&amp;#39;s intended use.&lt;/p&gt;\r\n\r\n&lt;p style="margin: 0.4em 0px 0.5em; line-height: 19.1875px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: sans-serif;"&gt;A distribution&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Desktop_Linux" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Desktop Linux"&gt;oriented toward desktop use&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;will typically include the&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/X_Window_System" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="X Window System"&gt;X Window System&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;and an accompanying&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Desktop_environment" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="GNOME"&gt;GNOME&lt;/a&gt;or&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/KDE_Plasma_Workspaces" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="KDE Plasma Workspaces"&gt;KDE Plasma&lt;/a&gt;. Some such distributions may include a less resource intensive desktop such as&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/LXDE" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="LXDE"&gt;LXDE&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;or&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Xfce" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Xfce"&gt;Xfce&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;for use on older or less powerful computers. A distribution intended to run as a server may omit all graphical environments from the standard install and instead include other software such as the&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Apache_HTTP_Server" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Apache HTTP Server"&gt;Apache HTTP Server&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;and an&amp;nbsp;&lt;a class="mw-redirect" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/SSH_server" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="SSH server"&gt;SSH server&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;such as&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OpenSSH" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="OpenSSH"&gt;OpenSSH&lt;/a&gt;. Because Linux is freely redistributable, anyone may create a distribution for any intended use. Applications commonly used with desktop Linux systems include the&amp;nbsp;&lt;a class="mw-redirect" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mozilla_Firefox" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Mozilla Firefox"&gt;Mozilla Firefox&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;web browser, the&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/LibreOffice" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="LibreOffice"&gt;LibreOffice&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;office application suite, and the&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/GIMP" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="GIMP"&gt;GIMP&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;image editor.&lt;/p&gt;\r\n', 10, '2013-05-02 17:39:41'),
