color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Navajo people"&gt;Navajo&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;people. Since the Navajo and the other Apache groups are clearly related through culture and language, they are all considered&amp;nbsp;&lt;b&gt;Apachean&lt;/b&gt;. Apachean peoples formerly ranged over eastern&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arizona" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Arizona"&gt;Arizona&lt;/a&gt;, northern&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mexico" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Mexico"&gt;Mexico&lt;/a&gt;,&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/New_Mexico" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="New Mexico"&gt;New Mexico&lt;/a&gt;, west and southwest&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Texas" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Texas"&gt;Texas&lt;/a&gt;, and southern&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Colorado" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Colorado"&gt;Colorado&lt;/a&gt;. The&amp;nbsp;&lt;a class="new" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Apacher%C3%ADa&amp;amp;action=edit&amp;amp;redlink=1" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(165, 88, 88); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Apacher&iacute;a (page does not exist)"&gt;Apacher&amp;iacute;a&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;consisted of high mountains, sheltered and watered valleys, deep canyons, deserts, and the southern&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Plains" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Great Plains"&gt;Great Plains&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;\r\n\r\n&lt;p style="margin: 0.4em 0px 0.5em; line-height: 19.1875px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: sans-serif;"&gt;The Apachean groups had little political unity; the major groups spoke seven different languages and developed distinct and competitive cultures. The current division of Apachean groups includes the Navajo,&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Western_Apache" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Western Apache"&gt;Western Apache&lt;/a&gt;,&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Chiricahua" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Chiricahua"&gt;Chiricahua&lt;/a&gt;,&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mescalero" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Mescalero"&gt;Mescalero&lt;/a&gt;,&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jicarilla_Apache" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Jicarilla Apache"&gt;Jicarilla&lt;/a&gt;,&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lipan_Apache_people" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Lipan Apache people"&gt;Lipan&lt;/a&gt;, and&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Plains_Apache" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Plains Apache"&gt;Plains Apache&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;(formerly Kiowa-Apache). Apache groups live in&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Oklahoma" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Oklahoma"&gt;Oklahoma&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;and&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Texas" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Texas"&gt;Texas&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;and on&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Indian_reservation" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Indian reservation"&gt;reservations&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;in Arizona and New Mexico.&lt;/p&gt;\r\n\r\n&lt;p style="margin: 0.4em 0px 0.5em; line-height: 19.1875px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: sans-serif;"&gt;Some Apacheans have moved to large metropolitan areas. The largest Apache urban communities are in&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Oklahoma_City" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; (20, 'ASP.NET MVC Framework', '&lt;p style="margin: 0.4em 0px 0.5em; line-height: 19.1875px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: sans-serif;"&gt;Based on&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ASP.NET" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="ASP.NET"&gt;ASP.NET&lt;/a&gt;, it allows software developers to build a&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Web_application" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Web application"&gt;web application&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;as a composition of three roles:&amp;nbsp;&lt;i&gt;Model&lt;/i&gt;,&amp;nbsp;&lt;i&gt;View&lt;/i&gt;&amp;nbsp;and&amp;nbsp;&lt;i&gt;Controller&lt;/i&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;\r\n\r\n&lt;p style="margin: 0.4em 0px 0.5em; line-height: 19.1875px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: sans-serif;"&gt;A&amp;nbsp;&lt;i&gt;model&lt;/i&gt;&amp;nbsp;represents the state of a particular aspect of the application. A&amp;nbsp;&lt;i&gt;controller&lt;/i&gt;&amp;nbsp;handles interactions and updates the model to reflect a change in state of the application, and then passes information to the view. A&amp;nbsp;&lt;i&gt;view&lt;/i&gt;&amp;nbsp;accepts necessary information from the controller and renders a user interface to display that information.&lt;sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-aspnetmvc_2-0" style="line-height: 1em;"&gt;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ASP.NET_MVC#cite_note-aspnetmvc-2" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; white-space: nowrap; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;"&gt;[2]&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/sup&gt;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n\r\n&lt;p style="margin: 0.4em 0px 0.5em; line-height: 19.1875px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: sans-serif;"&gt;In April 2009, the ASP.NET MVC source code was released under the&amp;nbsp;&lt;a class="mw-redirect" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Microsoft_Public_License" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Microsoft Public License"&gt;Microsoft Public License&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;(MS-PL).&lt;sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-opensource_3-0" style="line-height: 1em;"&gt;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ASP.NET_MVC#cite_note-opensource-3" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; white-space: nowrap; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;"&gt;[3]&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/sup&gt;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n\r\n&lt;p style="margin: 0.4em 0px 0.5em; line-height: 19.1875px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: sans-serif;"&gt;ASP.NET MVC framework is a lightweight, highly testable presentation framework that is integrated with existing ASP.NET features. Some of these integrated features are master pages and membership-based authentication. The MVC framework is defined in the System.Web.Mvc assembly.&lt;sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-4" style="line-height: 1em;"&gt;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ASP.NET_MVC#cite_note-4" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; white-space: nowrap; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;"&gt;[4]&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/sup&gt;&lt;/p&gt;\r\n\r\n&lt;p style="margin: 0.4em 0px 0.5em; line-height: 19.1875px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: sans-serif;"&gt;The ASP.NET MVC Framework couples the models, views, and controllers using&amp;nbsp;&lt;a class="mw-redirect" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Interface_(computer_science)" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Interface (computer science)"&gt;interface&lt;/a&gt;-based contracts, thereby allowing each component to be easily tested independently.&lt;/p&gt;\r\n', 5, '2013-05-02 17:54:57'),

(22, 'Algorithms + Data Structures = Programs', '&lt;p style="margin: 0.4em 0px 0.5em; line-height: 19.1875px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: sans-serif;"&gt;&lt;i&gt;&lt;b&gt;Algorithms + Data Structures = Programs&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/i&gt;&lt;sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-1" style="line-height: 1em;"&gt;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Algorithms_%2B_Data_Structures_%3D_Programs#cite_note-1" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; white-space: nowrap; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;"&gt;[1]&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/sup&gt;&amp;nbsp;is a 1976 book written by&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Niklaus_Wirth" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Niklaus Wirth"&gt;Niklaus Wirth&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;covering some of the fundamental topics of&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Computer_programming" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Computer programming"&gt;computer programming&lt;/a&gt;, particularly that&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Algorithm" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Algorithm"&gt;algorithms&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;and&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Data_structure" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Data structure"&gt;data structures&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;are inherently related. For example, if one has a&amp;nbsp;&lt;a class="mw-redirect" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sorted_list" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Sorted list"&gt;sorted list&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;one will use a&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Search_algorithm" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Search algorithm"&gt;search algorithm&lt;/a&gt;&amp;nbsp;optimal for sorted lists.&lt;/p&gt;\r\n\r\n&lt;p style="margin: 0.4em 0px 0.5em; line-height: 19.1875px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: sans-serif;"&gt;The book was one of the most influential computer science books of the time and, like Wirth&amp;#39;s other work, extensively used in education&lt;sup class="Template-Fact" style="line-height: 1em; white-space: nowrap;"&gt;[&lt;i&gt;&lt;a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" style="text-decoration: none; color: rgb(11, 0, 128); background-image: none; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial;" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"&gt;&lt;span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `comments` (
  `CommentID` bigint(20) unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `Ordinal` bigint(20) unsigned NOT NULL,
  `CommentDate` datetime NOT NULL,
  `Comment` text NOT NULL,
  `UserID` int(10) unsigned NOT NULL,
  `QuestionID` bigint(20) unsigned DEFAULT NULL,
  `AnswerID` bigint(20) unsigned DEFAULT NULL,
  `ArticleID` bigint(20) unsigned DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`CommentID`),
  KEY `fk_comments_answers` (`AnswerID`),
  KEY `fk_comments_questions` (`QuestionID`),
  KEY `fk_comments_articles` (`ArticleID`),
  KEY `fk_comments_users` (`UserID`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 AUTO_INCREMENT=1 ;

  `LogID` bigint(20) unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `UserID` int(10) unsigned NOT NULL,
  `LogDate` datetime NOT NULL,
  `AnswerID` bigint(20) unsigned DEFAULT NULL,
  `QuestionID` bigint(20) unsigned DEFAULT NULL,
  `ArticleID` bigint(20) unsigned DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`LogID`),
  KEY `fk_logs_users` (`UserID`),
  KEY `fk_logs_answers` (`AnswerID`),
  KEY `fk_logs_articles` (`ArticleID`),
  KEY `fk_logs_questions` (`QuestionID`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB  DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 AUTO_INCREMENT=2 ;

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `users` (
  `UserID` int(10) unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `FirstName` varchar(50) NOT NULL,

  `Password` varchar(32) NOT NULL,
  `Email` varchar(100) NOT NULL,
  `ProfilePicture` varchar(100) DEFAULT NULL,
  `PictureFolderLocation` varchar(100) DEFAULT NULL,
  `Location` varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL,
  `WebSite` varchar(100) DEFAULT NULL,
  `DateOfBirth` date DEFAULT NULL,
  `AboutSelf` text,
  `Sex` enum('m','f') NOT NULL,
  `RegistrationDate` datetime NOT NULL,
  `Key` varchar(64) NOT NULL,
  `ConfirmAccount` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `UserType` enum('admin','user') NOT NULL DEFAULT 'user',
  PRIMARY KEY (`UserID`),
  UNIQUE KEY `Email` (`Email`),
  UNIQUE KEY `Username` (`Username`),
  UNIQUE KEY `Key` (`Key`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB  DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 AUTO_INCREMENT=15 ;

ALTER TABLE `answers`
  ADD CONSTRAINT `fk_answers_questions` FOREIGN KEY (`QuestionID`) REFERENCES `questions` (`QuestionID`),
  ADD CONSTRAINT `fk_answers_users` FOREIGN KEY (`UserID`) REFERENCES `users` (`UserID`);


ALTER TABLE `articles`
  ADD CONSTRAINT `fk_articles_users` FOREIGN KEY (`UserID`) REFERENCES `users` (`UserID`);


ALTER TABLE `article_tags`
  ADD CONSTRAINT `fk_article_tags_articles` FOREIGN KEY (`ArticleID`) REFERENCES `articles` (`ArticleID`),
  ADD CONSTRAINT `fk_article_tags_tags` FOREIGN KEY (`TagID`) REFERENCES `tags` (`TagID`);


ALTER TABLE `comments`
  ADD CONSTRAINT `fk_comments_answers` FOREIGN KEY (`AnswerID`) REFERENCES `answers` (`AnswerID`),
  ADD CONSTRAINT `fk_comments_articles` FOREIGN KEY (`ArticleID`) REFERENCES `articles` (`ArticleID`),
  ADD CONSTRAINT `fk_comments_questions` FOREIGN KEY (`QuestionID`) REFERENCES `questions` (`QuestionID`),
  ADD CONSTRAINT `fk_comments_users` FOREIGN KEY (`UserID`) REFERENCES `users` (`UserID`);


ALTER TABLE `evaluation`
  ADD CONSTRAINT `evaluation_ibfk_1` FOREIGN KEY (`UserID`) REFERENCES `users` (`UserID`),
  ADD CONSTRAINT `evaluation_ibfk_2` FOREIGN KEY (`QuestionID`) REFERENCES `questions` (`QuestionID`),
  ADD CONSTRAINT `evaluation_ibfk_3` FOREIGN KEY (`ArticleID`) REFERENCES `articles` (`ArticleID`);


ALTER TABLE `follow_tags`
  ADD CONSTRAINT `fk_follow_tags_tags` FOREIGN KEY (`TagID`) REFERENCES `tags` (`TagID`),
  ADD CONSTRAINT `fk_follow_tags_users` FOREIGN KEY (`UserID`) REFERENCES `users` (`UserID`);


ALTER TABLE `logs`
  ADD CONSTRAINT `fk_logs_answers` FOREIGN KEY (`AnswerID`) REFERENCES `answers` (`AnswerID`),
  ADD CONSTRAINT `fk_logs_articles` FOREIGN KEY (`ArticleID`) REFERENCES `articles` (`ArticleID`),
  ADD CONSTRAINT `fk_logs_questions` FOREIGN KEY (`QuestionID`) REFERENCES `questions` (`QuestionID`),
  ADD CONSTRAINT `fk_logs_users` FOREIGN KEY (`UserID`) REFERENCES `users` (`UserID`);


ALTER TABLE `questions`
  ADD CONSTRAINT `fk_questions_users` FOREIGN KEY (`UserID`) REFERENCES `users` (`UserID`);


ALTER TABLE `question_tags`
  ADD CONSTRAINT `fk_question_tags_questions` FOREIGN KEY (`QuestionID`) REFERENCES `questions` (`QuestionID`),
  ADD CONSTRAINT `fk_question_tags_tags` FOREIGN KEY (`TagID`) REFERENCES `tags` (`TagID`);


ALTER TABLE `views`
  ADD CONSTRAINT `fk_views_articles` FOREIGN KEY (`ArticleID`) REFERENCES `articles` (`ArticleID`),
  ADD CONSTRAINT `fk_views_questions` FOREIGN KEY (`QuestionID`) REFERENCES `questions` (`QuestionID`),
  ADD CONSTRAINT `fk_views_users` FOREIGN KEY (`UserID`) REFERENCES `users` (`UserID`);


ALTER TABLE `votes`
  ADD CONSTRAINT `fk_votes_answers` FOREIGN KEY (`AnswerID`) REFERENCES `answers` (`AnswerID`),
  ADD CONSTRAINT `fk_votes_articles` FOREIGN KEY (`ArticleID`) REFERENCES `articles` (`ArticleID`),
  ADD CONSTRAINT `fk_votes_questions` FOREIGN KEY (`QuestionID`) REFERENCES `questions` (`QuestionID`),
  ADD CONSTRAINT `fk_votes_users` FOREIGN KEY (`UserID`) REFERENCES `users` (`UserID`);
